============================================================
-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

3xHeal
-------
3 times, use a random HP- and/or MP-restoring skill.

  (2/16 chance each)  Phoenix
  (1/16 chance each)  Cure, Cure 2, Cure 3, Heal Force, Ice Rabbit, Life, Life 2, Mantra, Pearl Wind, Sraphim, Starlet, Sun Bath, Tapir, Wild Bear

?-Beast
-------
??? times, use a random beast-summoning Dance move.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Cokatrice, Ice Rabbit, Kitty, Pois. Frog, Tapir, Whump, Wild Bear, Wombat

AerDisc
-------
Use the combo Aero + Dischord.

Blaster
-------
Use the skill 'Blaster'

Cure2
-------
Use the skill 'Cure 2'

R-Blitz
-------
Use a random Blitz.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Air Blade, AuraBolt, Bum Rush, Fire Dance, Mantra, Pummel, Spiraler, Suplex

R-Rare
-------
Use a random rare effect (Slots, Super Ball, non-Lore monster skill).
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Absolute 0, Bio Blaster, Blaster, Blaze, Blizzard, Dread, Evil Toot, Fire Ball, Fire Wall, Flash Rain, Goner, Grav Bomb, Imp Song, Lode Stone, Love Token, Lullaby, Magnitude8, Megahit, Megazerk, Mute, Overcast, R.Polarity, Raid, Revenger, Scar Beam, Slide, Slimer, Tek Laser, TekBarrier, Tentacle, Virite, WallChange

W-Sraph
-------
2 times, use the skill 'Sraphim'

-05- BLITZ INPUTS
------------------------------------------------------------
1. left, right, left
2. Y, X, Y, up
3. X, Y, R, right
4. Y, L, Y, X, R, L
5. right, up-right, up, up-left, left, R, X
6. left, right, right, right, right
7. left, up-left, up, down, up, up-right, right
8. left, down-left, down, up, down, up, L, X
